Looking for data from older rounds? I still have them!
What do all these numbers mean? The first five columns indicate the starting odds of each of the bets in the arenas. A "1" means not to bet in that arena. So, 3 1 2 2 2 means:

Current Bets
RoundBet InfoAmountOddsWinnings
7079Shipwreck: Ol' Stripey
Treasure Island: Ned the Skipper
Hidden Cove: Federismo Corvallio
Harpoon Harry's: Gooblah the Grarrl
13336 NP24:1320064 NP


Here, Ol' Stripey has 3:1 odds, and the others have 2:1. Hence, 24:1.
The sixth column represents the total odds, in this case, it's 24:1.
The seventh column represents the expected return for the bet. Meaning if you were to make the same bet in the same arena over and over again, you'd end up making that many NP divided by the amount of NP you spent.
The last columns indicate the pirates in a given arena to bet on. A "5" means not to bet in that arena. This is used to distinguish between two or more pirates in the same arena with the same odds.
